[09/12/24, 11:04:51‚ÄØAM] Anthony-Agent-Friendly Realtors: BRH Agent: *Proposal to Expand CREA(I) Membership Opportunities*

Hi Joe, Sameer, and Committee,  

During my recent interactions with International Real Estate Associations, I was intrigued to discover that they include professionals from diverse fields connected to real estate, such as Architects, Interior Designers, Chartered Accountants, Advocates, Banks, and Financial Institutions, Wealth Management, Relocation, Urban Planning, as active members.  

This approach not only enriches the association but also fosters collaboration and creates mutual benefits for all parties involved.  

I propose that the CREA(I) committee consider exploring similar opportunities to expand our membership base, focusing on fostering collaboration and creating a win-win scenario for all stakeholders.  

Looking forward to your thoughts & I'm more than happy to propose the Implementation Plan?

Best regards,  
Anthony
Friendly Realtors and Property Management
